<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the rating package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> rating</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/rating-group&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The rating package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:rating-group/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div <h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each rating part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the rating is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the
rating, control and label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;rating&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for rating disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for rating control disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for rating label disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="checked-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Checked State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#checked-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the rating is checked, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-checked</code> attribute is added to the rating
part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;rating&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-checked</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for rating checked state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="readonly-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Readonly State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#readonly-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the rating is readonly, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-readonly</code> attribute is added to the
rating part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;rating&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-readonly</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for rating readonly state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="highlighted" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a rating is highlighted, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute is added to the
rating part.</p>

<p>When a rating is half, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-half</code> attribute is added to the rating part.</p>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The rating group <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px rating group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the rating group</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the next star, increasing the rating value based on the `allowHalf` property.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the previous star, decreasing the rating value based on the `allowHalf` property.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div>Selects the focused star in the rating group.</div></li></ul><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/components/rating-group.mdx" item.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Rating\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Syncs with `disabled` state of `fieldset`\n- Supports form `reset` events\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the rating group package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"rating-group/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the rating anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the rating package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as rating from \"@zag-js/rating-group\"\n```\n\nThe rating package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"rating-group/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nUse the `defaultValue` property to set the rating's initial value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  defaultValue: 2.5,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled rating value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control the rating externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Setting and clearing value programmatically\n\nUse `api.setValue` or `api.clearValue` when you need imperative control.\n\n```jsx\napi.setValue(4)\napi.clearValue()\n```\n\n### Allowing half ratings\n\nEnable `allowHalf` when your UX needs fractional ratings.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  allowHalf: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for changes\n\nWhen the rating value changes, the `onValueChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  onValueChange({ value }) {\n    console.log(\"rating value is:\", value)\n    // 1 | 2.5 | 4\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for hover changes\n\nUse `onHoverChange` to react to hover previews before selection.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  onHoverChange(details) {\n    console.log(\"hovered rating:\", details.hoveredValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing screen reader value text\n\nUse `translations.ratingValueText` to customize how each rating item is\nannounced.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  translations: {\n    ratingValueText: (index) =\u003e `${index} out of 5`,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nTo use rating in forms, set `name` and render `api.getHiddenInputProps()`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rating.machine, {\n  name: \"rating\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach rating part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the rating is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the\nrating, control and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"rating\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for rating disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for rating control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for rating label disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Checked State\n\nWhen the rating is checked, the `data-checked` attribute is added to the rating\npart.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"rating\"][data-checked] {\n  /* styles for rating checked state */\n}\n```\n\n### Readonly State\n\nWhen the rating is readonly, the `data-readonly` attribute is added to the\nrating part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"rating\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* styles for rating readonly state */\n}\n```\n\n### Highlighted\n\nWhen a rating is highlighted, the `data-highlighted` attribute is added to the\nrating part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"rating\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for highlighted rating */\n}\n```\n\n### Half rating\n\nWhen a rating is half, the `data-half` attribute is added to the rating part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"rating\"][data-half] {\n  /* styles for half rating */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe rating group machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe rating group `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"rating-group\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Rating Group\",\"description\":\"Using the
